  <span id="freeText13506992492729093079" style="display:none"><b>Reread Review November 14,2017</b><br /><br />I LOVE this book. It's a little quirky, the writing is a bit strange. It's completely unrealistic, most "humans" are the ultimate evil bad guys, BUT I JUST LOVE THIS whole series; and this one starts it all. The New Species people are just so endearing. They have been keeping human test subjects chained and emprisioned treating them like less than animals. Ellie is working undercover to try and gain evidence for the government to go in and save theses people but has become odsesses with one particular prisoner. She watches and dreams about him and saving him has become her true mission.<br />While watching the object of her obsession one day through a two way mirror she sees one of the technicians about to abuse him in the worst way or maybe even kill him and she has to stop him. She kills the tech but has to leave the prisoner (it turns out to be Fury but I can't remember his number) to take the blame because she has finialy gathered the evidence she needs to free him and the other prisoners and can't take a chance of being caught. Of course Fury thinks she has just abandoned him to take the blame and punishment for the crime she committed and feels especially decieved because she was always so kind to him before. Months later when he sees that she works at Homeland (the home that was given to the New Species people by the US gov after they were rescued fom Mercile) he wants to kill her or does he...<br />I loved it. <span id="freeTextContainer8388517889919738811">5 Fury Stars <br/><br/>I first read this book in 2013; I have read it since one more time. And I had started a few books that just didn't hold my interest. Not because they were bad but my mind is just so on Christmas stuff. <br/><br/>So I thought what book can I just zone out while doing all my Christmas errands and this was the book I choose. I forgot how much I love Fury, he is so big and strong and protective <3 <br/><br/>Ellie is so good and sweet and wants to be good and do good. I love this world Laurann created. Home</span>
  <span id="freeText8388517889919738811" style="display:none">5 Fury Stars <br /><br />I first read this book in 2013; I have read it since one more time. And I had started a few books that just didn't hold my interest. Not because they were bad but my mind is just so on Christmas stuff. <br /><br />So I thought what book can I just zone out while doing all my Christmas errands and this was the book I choose. I forgot how much I love Fury, he is so big and strong and protective &lt;3 <br /><br />Ellie is so good and sweet and wants to be good and do good. I love this world Laurann created. Homeland is like a magical place to me. Where the rescued can be free and be themselves who would want that for the New Species? <br /><br />When I first read about this series I thought hmm maybe not for me, but then I thought give it a try you just never know and I am so very glad I did. It’s one of my most favorite series to date<br /><br />Vanessa Chambers does a fabulous job narrating this unique series, she bring each character to life with their own voice. I am so glad she does the whole series! <br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1458797478?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aileene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aileene" href="/user/show/4150124-aileene">Aileene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4150124-aileene?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1458797478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17770773017183489664">BR-ing this with my lovely gal pal <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/photo/user/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-lpc-nynaeve' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jess</a> today 7 Dec.<br/><br/>Would this be as good as the Not-Hoth blue aliens series? LETS FIND OUT!<br/><br/>And I did find out...<br/><br/>Hey, you! <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368514.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yes, you, Not-Hoth blue aliens...this is for you, boys!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368515.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>*faces the other side and gushes*<br/><b> Well, hello New Species! </b><br/><br/>I liked the book - end of review.<br/>Giving it 3.5 stars<br/>.......<br/><br/>.......<br/><br/>.......<br/><br/>Alright. Alright. Before I get <b> more </b> pointed stares and raised eyebrows, no, I'm not ditching my blue aliens. I have invested too much emotions on my Not-Hot</span>
  <span id="freeText17770773017183489664" style="display:none">BR-ing this with my lovely gal pal <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/photo/user/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-lpc-nynaeve" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a> today 7 Dec.<br><br>Would this be as good as the Not-Hoth blue aliens series? LETS FIND OUT!<br><br>And I did find out...<br><br>Hey, you! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368514.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, you, Not-Hoth blue aliens...this is for you, boys!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368515.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>*faces the other side and gushes*<br><b> Well, hello New Species! </b><br><br>I liked the book - end of review.<br>Giving it 3.5 stars<br>.......<br><br>.......<br><br>.......<br><br>Alright. Alright. Before I get <b> more </b> pointed stares and raised eyebrows, no, I'm not ditching my blue aliens. I have invested too much emotions on my Not-Hoth hotties that I just can't ignore them that easily. This book (of New Species) had come really close though.<br><br>First installment is the story of Fury whom I found really sexy (at times - only at times. And other times, he's annoying plus!) but not his name. I hate his name.<br>He was <s> born </s> an experiment made from human and animal DNA combined. He lived in a cell and was abused in so many ways by people around him. <br>Ellie, the heroine, was hired to gather information about the company where Fury and his other species were confined.<br>Whilst Ellie was spying, she saw Fury and felt something for him.<br><br>After monthS, she finally acquired the information she needed but one situation gone wrong and she needed to save Fury. And that's where basically the story started. <br><br><u> What didn't work for me. </u><br>--&gt; The first quarter of the book was annoyingly wasted on Fury wanting revenge on the day Ellie saved him and Ellie's non stop explaining the truth behind of what she has done then followed by endless apologies.<br><b> SERIOUSLY, ONE 'SPLAININ' WAS ENOUGH. MOVE ON ALREADY! </b><br><br>--&gt; Whilst I adore males going alpha on their females, Fury on the other hand doesn't believe in moderation. He was f*cking annoying when he goes overboard.<br><br>--&gt; Justice North (blech!) I know he means well but wtf! he needs to take a chill pill and needs to back the f* off. <br><br><u> What did work for me. </u><br>--&gt; The story. Way too much drama that I thought there was no ending but (I think) it was executed well that my attention didn't wander elsewhere.<br><br>--&gt; Breeze. I want to get to know her. I want to read her story.<br><br>--&gt; Trisha Norbit. She intrigues me and her intentions. I like her but my gut thinks differently. <br><br>--&gt; And of course, THIS.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368516.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Who needs just ridges when you can have this too?<br><i> "Our cocks swell right as we ejaculate. It’s nature’s way of locking a male inside a female at the end of sex with some species." </i><br><u> THEY AIN'T NO MINUTE MAN! </u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368517.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WAIT A MINUTE.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368518.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450009048ra/17368519.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Rating it <b> 3.5 </b> <i> I-want-ridges-and-this-new-found-lock-in-intensifiers </i> <b> Stars </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17770773017183489664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Sh9PheTZ9CnBYYNP6IMfQ5k/CResOmCoz+OCDfRPMi7o1C4owsmj2QBgUobLa1p/DHjZ8X1iAsUxSW1hkdgIQw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zf4uDIDkR8w4mRt5oGDPszWSWW4wYIvaxZuzkMBBmWhvNU+hpvQQPPmYyrCDiIqPoNWJiOE46bc7MVz8pdajBQ==')})

          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/3190846.Laurann_Dohner"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1285546473p3/3190846.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/3190846.Laurann_Dohner">Laurann Dohner

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13730791144263133567">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText13730791144263133567" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13730791144263133567" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

It will break her heart but she must walk away.\n\nMoon has been drugged, his memory shattered, and he’s now little more than feral, a dangerous threat to everyone. In their need for help, the NSO doctors turn to the only female Moon ever cared about—the one who left him behind two years ago.\n\nMoon isn’t the same male Joy once knew. There are no rules now. If sex tames the wild beast and triggers his fractured memories, allowing him moments of lucidity, then Joy will give him everything, body and soul. She’ll do whatever it takes to save him—even at the cost of her own life.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"2598943807720138979\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return       <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/17030827-fury">Quotes from Fury</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;You are ours and he should have known not to touch you."<br /><br />"I'm yours? I thought you hated me."<br /><br />Kit stepped out of the bathroom. "We don't hate you. You're our pet."<br /><br />"Kit!" Rusty shook her head. "Don't say that. You'll offend her."<br /><br />Kit shrugged "She is. She's so little and cute. She yaps around trying to please like... What are they called? A Yorkie?"<br /><br />Rusty sighed. "We decided she's more similar to a cute little poodle with her long blonde hair." She flashed a smile at Ellie. "Don't take it offensively please. We enjoy having you around and you amuse us to no end.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/712674-you-are-ours-and-he-should-have-known-not-to">54 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Mooch? What does that word mean?”<br /><br />Ellie smiled. “It’s a term when you live with someone and take something freely from the person who has to work for it. It’s not a good thing. It’s hard to explain that one. I guess I could describe it as I’m a burden to him.”<br /><br />“How? He already had a room you could have.”<br /><br />Ellie struggled with her thoughts. Some words were hard to explain. “Yes. He did but usually you don’t live with someone unless you are a couple. Then it is acceptable if you share food and a home. If you aren’t, then both parties are supposed to work, similar to a partnership, be equal. I am not his girlfriend or his partner. He provides a home and food for me while I give him nothing in return. I’m a mooch.”<br /><br />“I think I understand.” Breeze smiled. “And you are not a mooch. He doesn’t know what one is so therefore you can’t be what he doesn’t know exists.&rdquo;</span>
